            addeśarātramāsīta | kiñcid dātātapapavanam āseveta | punaś cāntaḥ praviśet | na cātmānam
              ādarśe<pb n="286r"/><unclear>syu</unclear>vā nirīkṣeta | rūpaśālitvāt tato 'nyad
            addaśarātraṃ krodhādīn pariharet | eṣa sarvveṣām upayogaḥ | viśeṣatas tu
              vallīpratāna<unclear>kṣu</unclear>pādayaḥ somā bhakṣayitavyāḥ | bhavanti<lb n="2"/>
            teṣām arthacaturthāmuṣṭayaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.29.13">aṃśumantaṃ sauvarṇṇapātre 'bhiṣuyā<cb/>yāccandramasaṃ rājate | tāv
            upayojyāṣṭaguṇam aiśvaryam avāpyaiś ānandevam paśyati | śeṣās tu tāmra<pb n="3"/> maye

              vrajedi<lb n="4"/>ti ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.3">do<cb/>ṣāḥ kṣīṇā bṛṃhayitavyāḥ | calitāḥ praśamayitavyāḥ |

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.5">tad yathāturaṃ snigdhasvinnamanabhiṣyandibhir ā<lb n="4"
            />hārairanavabaddhadoṣamālocya svo<add place="below-margin"><unclear>sto</unclear></add>
            vamanam pāyayitāsmīti<cb/>sambhojayet | sambhojyas tu tīkṣṇāgnir balavān bahudoṣo
            mahāvyādhiparigṛhīto vamanasātmyaś ca ||<lb n="5"/></l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.6">peśalair vvividhairannair doṣamutkliśya dehinaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             snigdhasvi<cb/>nnāya vamanan dattaṃ samyak pravarttate ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.4.33.7">athāparedyuḥ pūrvvāhṇe sādhāraṇe kāle vamanadravyakaṣāya<lb n="6"
            />kalkacūrṇṇasnehenānyatamasya mātrām pāyayitvā vāmayet |
            asātmyabībhatsadurddarśanadurggandhāni vāmanīyāni vidadhyāt ato viparītāni virecanāni |
            tatra suku<pb n="295v"/>mārāṃ kṛśāṃ bālaṃ vṛddhāṃ bhīrum vā vamanasādhyavikāreṣu
            kṣīradadhitakrayavāgūnāmanyatamamākaṇṭham pāyayitvā vāmayet | pītauṣadhañ ca pāṇibhir

             sadāhaśūlaṃṃ kṛcchreṇa kaphan tatropaveśyate |</l>

            <caesura/>
             sarppir madhukasiddhañ ca tailam vāpy anuvāsanaṃ |</l>

            <caesura/>
             sarvvadoṣaharaṃ bastiṃ śodhanaṃ tatra dāpayet |</l>

            <caesura/>

            <caesura/>
